\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00538}00538 \textcolor{comment}{// Writes two-\/digit numbers a, b and c separated by sep to buf.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00539}00539 \textcolor{comment}{// The method by Pavel Novikov based on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00540}00540 \textcolor{comment}{// https://johnnylee-\/sde.github.io/Fast-\/unsigned-\/integer-\/to-\/time-\/string/.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00541}00541 \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} write\_digit2\_separated(\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* buf, \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} b,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00542}00542                                    \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} c, \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} sep) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00543}00543   \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} digits =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00544}00544       a | (b << 24) | (static\_cast<unsigned long long>(c) << 48);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00545}00545   \textcolor{comment}{// Convert each value to BCD.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00546}00546   \textcolor{comment}{// We have x = a * 10 + b and we want to convert it to BCD y = a * 16 + b.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00547}00547   \textcolor{comment}{// The difference is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00548}00548   \textcolor{comment}{//   y -\/ x = a * 6}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00549}00549   \textcolor{comment}{// a can be found from x:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00550}00550   \textcolor{comment}{//   a = floor(x / 10)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00551}00551   \textcolor{comment}{// then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00552}00552   \textcolor{comment}{//   y = x + a * 6 = x + floor(x / 10) * 6}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00553}00553   \textcolor{comment}{// floor(x / 10) is (x * 205) >> 11 (needs 16 bits).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00554}00554   digits += (((digits * 205) >> 11) \& 0x000f00000f00000f) * 6;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00555}00555   \textcolor{comment}{// Put low nibbles to high bytes and high nibbles to low bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00556}00556   digits = ((digits \& 0x00f00000f00000f0) >> 4) |}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00557}00557            ((digits \& 0x000f00000f00000f) << 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00558}00558   \textcolor{keyword}{auto} usep = \textcolor{keyword}{static\_cast<}\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} \textcolor{keywordtype}{long}\textcolor{keyword}{>}(sep);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00559}00559   \textcolor{comment}{// Add ASCII '0' to each digit byte and insert separators.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00560}00560   digits |= 0x3030003030003030 | (usep << 16) | (usep << 40);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00561}00561 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00562}00562   \textcolor{keyword}{constexpr} \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} len = 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00563}00563   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (const\_check(is\_big\_endian())) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00564}00564     \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} tmp[len];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00565}00565     memcpy(tmp, \&digits, len);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00566}00566     std::reverse\_copy(tmp, tmp + len, buf);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00567}00567   \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00568}00568     memcpy(buf, \&digits, len);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00569}00569   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00570}00570 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l00571}00571 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l01005}01005   \textcolor{comment}{// do if the year is negative or exceeds 9999. Use the convention that \%C}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l01006}01006   \textcolor{comment}{// concatenated with \%y yields the same output as \%Y, and that \%Y contains at}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l01007}01007   \textcolor{comment}{// least 4 characters, with more only if necessary.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l01477}01477   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} num \% den == 0}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{bundled_2chrono_8h_source_l01479}01479              : (n > 18 ? 6 : count\_fractional\_digits(num * 10, den, n + 1));}
